def f(n):
 # Initialize variables:
 n_0 = 0
 n_1 = -1
 n_2 = 1
 n_3 = 0

 # Iterate n times:
 for i in range(n):
  # Multiply n_0 by 2:
  n_0 *= 2
  
  # Multiply n_1 by 2:
  n_1 *= 2
  
  # Add 2 to n_2:
  n_2 += 2
  
  # Add 1 to n_3:
  n_3 += 1

 return [n_0, n_1, n_2, n_3]

# Test the function with n = 10:
